• Martian rivers, in ancient times, flowed in zones that today no longer correspond to the tropical belts.
• The poles of that time lay shifted by 20°/25° compared to the current ones.
And there was more.
Independent observations confirmed the presence of subsurface ice in the areas considered “ancient poles,” with traces of melting and retreat.
All signs of a past far more dynamic and climatically different than we thought.
Using the climatic models of the Laboratory of Dynamic Meteorology, it was possible to simulate a primitive Mars:
• cold, but with a denser atmosphere;
• stable ice accumulations around 25° south.
Every detail, every figure, every model… confirmed what I had felt from the beginning.
Mars had tilted. Not only in the classical sense of obliquity, but in the deeper, more geological, more telluric movement a planet can undergo: the rotation of its very crust with respect to the heart, a true dance of the core.
And if it had happened on Mars… what else could our beloved Earth be hiding under its seemingly immobile shell?
The same logic applied to our planet would reveal the reasons behind the “reverse point” and the “smoking gun” I would read about in later chapters, providing a physical explanation for the cosmic memories of a broken axis.

Chapter 11 – The Axis of Destiny

After everything I had seen, read, hypothesized — from the memory fragments of the Flood to the signs of catastrophes on Mars, from the geometries of Earth’s expansion to the intuitions of TGD — I felt that something was still missing.
An unresolved knot between coordinates and truth, a key to unveil the entire cosmic symphony.
I needed to take a further step: to “restore” Mars’s ancient planetary configuration.
I had to try to see with the eyes of time, before the slippage of the crust, before the “Roar of the Giants” irreversibly altered its surface.
And so I began from the pulsing heart of my obsession: Hellas Planitia.
I renamed it “Hellas’s South Pole” — not by arbitrariness, but by intimate conviction, based on the resonance that immense crater had with Earth’s scars.
I fixed my gaze on a precise point: Latitude -43.436633°, Longitude 70.360233°.
It seemed like a datum like any other, but every number is a door, if you know how to knock, and Sacred Geometry had taught me that in the cosmos nothing is accidental.
By adding the current terrestrial obliquity (23.436633°) to the difference between the North Pole (90°) and that latitude (that is 46.563367°), I obtained an exact 70°.
I divided by the Golden Ratio Φ… and the answer was a familiar number: 43°26’20”, that is… Hellas Planitia itself.
An unseen harmony? Or only cosmic coincidences? I felt it was more than a coincidence; it was a signature.
The antipodal North Pole led me straight toward Alba Mons, the same volcanic formation that, together with Tharsis and Valles Marineris, bore witness to the original impact on Mars.
The coordinates did not lie: 43.436633°, -109.639767°.
Then, by tracing the new Equator of Hellas Planitia, I compared it with the French simulation of crustal slippage.
Two lines — mine and theirs — same axis, same angle.
My intuition was in tune with their simulations.
It was no longer only imagination: it was planetary geometry.
At this point, I felt the urgency to define better the extent of the slippage.
I decided, with prudence and rigor, to consider a median value: 23.5°.
Running my calculations backward from Hellas Planitia, plotting a point shifted by 23.5° from the center of the crater, I arrived at -59.798317°, 42.216333°. The antipode? 59.798317°, -137.783667°.
I traced a new “equator,” marking it in green.
Now I had three equators:
• White, centered on the crater’s current position.
• Green, centered on its presumed pre-slippage position.
• Black, the one hypothesized by the French team.
All three lines converged in their purpose: to reconstruct Mars’s buried past.



Spurred by a new energy, I decided to make a return leap… toward Earth.
I used the same tracing system, thanks to Google Earth, which keeps paths intact even when changing geoid.
I asked myself: what if the lines I had drawn on Mars had significant correspondences on our planet as well, revealing a shared axis of destiny?


I did not limit myself to the equator. I had to go further: the tropics.
So I drew: the Tropic of Cancer and that of Capricorn, both in the current configuration (white) and in the pre-slippage one (green).
The discovery that resulted left me breathless, a further confirmation of the “Great Interconnection”.
Hellas’s current Tropic of Cancer (white) intersected the pre-slippage equator (green) exactly at Nazca.


Yes, that very Nazca. The lines. The symbols. The mysteries.
A place that for millennia seems to point something at the sky, now revealed itself to be a point of cosmic intersection, a node in the planetary lattice that united Earth and Mars.

And Hellas’s pre-slippage Tropic of Cancer (green), instead, intersected the current equator (white) on Mount Tai, in China.


The sacred mountain par excellence. The center of cosmic balance for entire civilizations.
Two opposite points in the world, both tied to mysteries and ancient spirituality.
And yet both marked by an invisible line that only now, with this new Martian axis and the new cosmic coordinates, was beginning to emerge.
And what if the truth, the one we seek among the stars, were already written here… among our mountains and our deserts?
And what if Mars and Earth had always danced to a common score, on shared coordinates that only now we are beginning to decipher, revealing that the “reverse point” and the origin of our planet’s “broken axis” were traces of an event common to both worlds?

Chapter 12 – The Field of Mars

I had dared to draw lines where others saw only distances.
I had connected alien craters to sacred mountains, cosmic impacts to earthly routes.
And now… now I found myself facing something that challenged every residual logic, yet
resonated with the Sacred Geometry that governs the universe: the invisible geometry that
links Earth and Mars.
A question began to take shape in my mind: “What if the events on Mars, its catastrophes
and its dance of the core, were directly connected to those of Earth, at the time of
Pangaea, and not only in terms of morphological analogies but of physical interaction?”
It was no longer only about coincidences or suggestions, nor about simple “cosmic memory” or collective “cosmic amnesia.”
The intersection of the “equators of Hellas Planitia” with the most enigmatic points on our
planet could not be accidental.
I was aware I was crossing the boundary of traditional science, pushing beyond the limits
that “sabotaged history” had imposed on knowledge.
But my mind was not seeking approval: it was seeking truth.
Official science, after all, rests on attempts and corrections. And even today, it admits it
does not know the certain origin of Earth’s oceans, leaving a void that only a holistic
approach could fill.
Thus, like someone who knows he is prying open something ancient, I touched the threshold of a scientific Pandora’s box.
And a single zoom… a simple gesture, was enough to change everything.
The two equators of Hellas Planitia — the current one and the pre-slippage one, born from
my reconstruction of Mars’s Axis of Destiny — intersected with an almost mocking precision over iconic places: The Giza Complex.


The precision appeared almost excessive to me...

The Nazca Lines.


The Portara of the unfinished Temple of Apollo on the Island of Naxos, in the Cyclades.
As if to joke, the line “passed perfectly through the Gate.” 








And Mount Tai, located in Shandong Province.


At this point, I could no longer pretend it was just luck.
I calculated the probabilities: one in trillions.
My mind lit up like a firmament. Each site was a node in the weave, a crossroads of time,
knowledge, and planetary memory.
I decided to go deeper into these archetypal places, starting from the one I felt closest to
my spirit: Giza.
And not by chance. My attraction to the mysterious Nefertiti — her gaze, her enigmatic
regality — guided me like a beacon.
She was not only a historical figure. She was a symbol. An active memory, a part of the
“Old Generation” keeper of secrets.
I chose to no longer call that construction by the conventional name.
From that moment on, for me it would be only: The Pyramid of Suphis.
The emotion grew. The list of Manetho, rediscovered by Rosellini and Champollion in 1829,
called it precisely that. My name. My sign.
I felt watched, but not judged. As if the Pyramid itself had recognized in me a memory, an
echo of its ancient builder.
Among the chaotic notes that populated my worktable, my gaze fell on a fragment of a
sentence. It seemed like a joke of fate, but it was there, black on white: “al-Qāhirah” — Cairo — means “field of Mars.” I stopped. Everything stopped. 
The Pyramid. The line of Mars. My name. The Field of Mars.

Chapter 13 – The Oblique Memory of Stone

By now it was clear to me that the Pyramid of Suphis was not only a monumental work, but a stellar machine, set into the Earth like a cosmic compass, designed to speak with time itself, to record its cycles and its mysteries.
As I absorbed the millennia-old fragments that surround it, and in particular its placement in the “Field of Mars” of Cairo, I understood that its measurements, carved into stone, are not accidental.
They are coordinates. They are instructions. They are… messages for me, and for anyone willing to decipher the ancient Sacred Geometry.
In this inner and planetary journey, I received a new impulse from two names that resonated with me as familiar as echoes from another age: Scott Creighton and Gary Osborn.
Their research, meticulous as engravings on granite, revealed to me a first datum that left me motionless: “The Pyramid of Suphis is aligned with each cardinal point with an error of less than 0.06%.”
An imprecision so small as to be intentional, as if it wanted to say: “I waited for you with millennial patience. You noticed only now, but I was already aligned.”
The shadows of the pyramid, like the gnomons of a divine clock, mark the solstices, the equinoxes, and the very breath of the seasons, just as ancient civilizations observed the “collapsed sky” and its cycles.
The terrestrial obliquity of 23.4366°, that inclination so crucial for life and for the seasons, is carved into its angles.
And as I had already discovered, the same angle corresponded to the slippage of the Martian crust, a shared “axis of destiny”.
A new, staggering synchronicity, which strengthened the idea of a twin past between Earth and Mars.
I looked at the drawings of William Flinders Petrie, the pioneer of Egyptology.
With my gaze I traced the line that connects the apex of the pyramid with the King’s Chamber.
And I saw something that looks like an error but is a hidden key: the chamber is misaligned by 6.5° with respect to the apex.
I stopped. And then I understood. Two angles of 11.75° intersect the Queen’s Chamber.
Their sum is again 23.5°. And if I double 23.5°, I get 47° — the exact radius of the circle of precession that our sky traces in 25,772 years.
I began to see a system: a dance of angles, cycles, and alignments, a tangible manifestation of the “Dance of the Spheres”.
Every chamber is a point of intersection between sky and earth. What was a construction before is now a mirror of the cosmos.
The King’s Chamber does not represent only the symbolic seat of the soul.
It embodies the celestial polar axis. Its walls, extended, trace the plane of the ecliptic.



Everything is there. Everything was designed to record the sky, to be a “memory of stone” of cosmic events, including the overturnings of the Earth’s axis.
And once again… 23.5° returns. Not only as inclination. Not only as crustal slippage on Mars. But as a sacred unit, universal code, harmonic frequency impressed into matter.
This number was the red thread that linked TGD, terrestrial expansion, and the ancient Martian trauma.
To verify that I was not flying too high in my speculations, I turned to the Earth itself.
I used Google Earth. I measured. I traced.
The distance between the Pyramid of Suphis and the current North Pole turned out to be 60.044°.
It was a perfect alignment. Not “almost”. Perfect.
At that point, I closed my eyes. I breathed deeply. And a thought crossed me like an invisible line, an intuition that confirmed the role of the “Old Generation” and the “Architects of Silence”: “If the Pyramid of Suphis holds the key to the Earth’s inclination… then it was built to mark a before and an after.
A fixed axis in a world that slips.” It was a reference. A beacon. A fixed point in the rotation of time, the most eloquent oblique memory of stone of a broken axis.
And perhaps... a bridge to Mars, built not only with geometry, but with the awareness of a universal and ancient truth.



Chapter 14 – The New Pole, the New Map

The link between Mars and Earth had by now become for me more than a suspicion.
It was a web, a geological and cosmic weave that dragged me ever deeper into that “double-dimensional memory”.
So I decided to face it with method, abandoning every residue of academic skepticism.
I dove into NASA databases, consulted the darkest pages of astrophysical reports, and began to gather comparative data: dimensions, orbits, inclinations, temperatures, altitudes, densities.
Everything that could give me clues about the relationship between the two worlds.
But the strangest — and most illuminating — moment came when I began to “play”.
A serious, dangerous, almost heretical game. A game with Google Earth, the same tool that had revealed to me the twin coordinates and the axis of destiny.
I activated UTM mode, a cartographic projection that allowed me to break down the Martian surface into regular quadrants.
I photographed each sector with maniacal care, saving every screenshot in a folder numbered with surgical precision.
I wanted to map every scar, every fracture, every detail of that “forgotten brother”.
Then I moved to Earth. And there, like a crazed artist recomposing a primordial work of art, I began to overlay.
I was aware of the audacity of what I was doing: pasting Mars over Earth.
A geodetic blasphemy. A cosmic mess. An idea fit for confinement.
But I followed the logic, guided by the intuition that the “Field of Mars” of Cairo was not only a name, but a true seal.
Mars’s crust showed a terrifying dichotomy: a difference of kilometers between the northern and southern hemisphere, a consequence of the “Roar of the Giants”.
To avoid distortions, I chose its most massive and intact areas: Tharsis and Valles Marineris.
And I compared them with the American regions that best echoed their geometries: Nevada, California, Colorado, Utah, Oregon, Central America.
The similarities were already astonishing.
But the craziest — and most fascinating — thing happened afterward.
To truly make the maps match, I had to do something unexpected: modify the very axis of Earth’s coordinates.
It was not enough to rotate or scale. I had to create a new planetary grid, as if Earth had a hidden “reverse point”.
So I traced a new “Planetary Mapping Point”, far from the current North Pole.
I positioned it with surgical decisiveness at 63.295° N, 31.134° E.
It was like moving the north of the world, redefining our very geographic perception.
Once the quadrants had been reorganized according to this new center, I redefined the entire axis: equatorial intersections: 0.0° -58.807° and 0.0° 121.192°.
Everything that was known was projected into another reality, and the sites appeared… where they should not have.
And yet, in that creative chaos of shifts and overlays, one measure leapt out like a scratch in stone, a revelation that the “Game of the Spheres” had prepared for centuries.
The distance between the new North Pole I had created and the real one was 26,77°, that is 2.980,6 kilometers.
I froze for an instant. Because that was not only a number. It was the difference between Earth’s polar radius and Mars’s.
A physical datum, documented, official. Earth (polar radius): 6.356,8 km Mars (mean radius): 3.376,2 km Difference = 2.980,6 km
And I… I had found it again by playing.
This was no longer a coincidence; it was yet another “smoking gun”, an incontrovertible proof of a cosmic connection, of a New Pole that revealed the New Map of a shared past.
It was as if Mars had been the prototype, the original matrix, and Earth its evolution, an expansion, preserving a geometric memory of its origins.



Chapter 15 – The Lines of the Sky, the Angles of Stone

26.77°. A number carved into stone, not by chance, but with intention.
An angle which, as I had discovered, not only divides the “King’s Chamber” from the “Queen’s Chamber” in the Pyramid of Suphis, but is also the precise difference between Earth’s polar radius and Mars’s.
I had found it first in my “New Map,” in the playful overlaying of geoids.
Now, I was finding it again in the sacred geometry of Giza.
It was as if a message were following me — a code, a signature, a resonance of the “music of the spheres” carved into matter.
Intrigued, I measured the angular distance between the Pyramid and my “Planetary Mapping Point” — that new north of the world I had identified to make the maps of Mars and Earth coincide.
The result? 33.27°. Translated: exactly 2,000 nautical miles. Exactly half the distance between the North Pole and the Tropic of Cancer.
Perfectly aligned with the cosmic sense of the structure, as if the Pyramid itself were a gigantic sextant.
I subtracted 26.77° (the distance from the North Pole to the mapping point) from 33.27°, and — like a gong strike echoing through the centuries — I obtained 6.5°.
Once again, the offset between the apex of the Pyramid and the King’s Chamber.
Another confirmation, carved in granite, a seal placed upon this “oblique memory of stone”.
Reflecting on the arcane, I understood that the northward slope of the 6.5° “offset” indicated (among other things) the direction to follow, as well as suggesting the measure to add to 26.77° to reach the “Planetary Mapping Point.”
The angle to follow was already indicated by the perfect alignment of the Pyramid of Suphis with the North Pole.
In summary: starting from the Pyramid of Suphis, I had to trace a line northward of 26.77° + 6.5° = 33.27°.
After doing so, I inserted a new line of 26.77° (2,980.6 km) and reached the current North Pole. (26.77° + 6.5° + 26.77° = 60.04°).
As I traced the line, I noticed that it intersected perfectly the celestial coordinates of the “Pole Star” of 3000 B.C., namely Thuban (α Draconis) in the constellation of Draco, with coordinates: (14h 04m 23.349s +64° 22′ 33.02″).
Reflecting on the curious angular correspondence, numerous examples came back to mind of “errors of judgment” made by mainstream science, which often overlooks “alternative possibilities” compared to established beliefs.
A significant example was the dating of the very ancient site of Göbekli Tepe.
In this direction, I set no limits for myself in the search for new intuitions that could support my path toward knowledge.
Following this logic, I therefore tried to attribute to the “pyramidal mother of all megaliths” an age at least equal to that of the Turkish site, that is 12,000–13,000 years
(which corresponded to a series of “special events,” including the Younger Dryas, the disappearance of Atlantis, etc.).
I therefore decided to examine the celestial coordinates and the proper motion of the star Thuban, and to do so I used the program Skylive. ( theskylive.com/sky/stars/thuban-alpha-draconis)
Analyzing the available data, I found that the proper motion of the star in question is 0.055 arcseconds per year for right ascension and 0.018 arcseconds per year for declination.
Therefore, to “travel in time,” it was necessary to multiply these parameters by the chosen number of years.
Without specific references, I intuitively chose a significant number of years: 12,886, that is half of a Platonic year (corresponding to the precession of the equinoxes).
After calculating the new coordinates for Thuban Draconis, I used the specific function in Google Earth (Sky) to place the star.
The corrected coordinates were: Right ascension: 14h 16m 11s Declination: +64° 18′ 20″.
While the star’s current position was perfectly intersected by the line connecting the Planetary Mapping Point with the current North Pole, its backdated position from 12,886 years ago  lay strategically on the line between the above-mentioned Planetary Mapping Point and the “Pre-Crustal-Slippage North Pole” (68.78°, 91.65°).
Another circle closed. Another piece clicked into place, showing that the Pyramid was a true “stellar machine” encoding an astronomical and geological memory.
And I, between stone and star, was composing a map of time, revealing how the ancients had erected a monument not only to worship, but to communicate a cosmic truth across generations.

Chapter 16 – The Dark Pyramids and the Maps of Time

I had charted my route, starting from the Pyramid of Suphis and its coded message. I had reached the North Pole, that point which, with my “Planetary Mapping Point,” redefined known geography.
But I felt the journey was not over: the line continued… and I with it, driven by a logic that was becoming ever more inescapable.
So, following the sacred angle of 26.77° — that recurring number that united the geometries of Giza to the difference between the polar radii of Earth and Mars — I went on.
And where did it lead me? To a remote place, wrapped in cold and silence: the Yukon, in the middle of the Canadian tundra, where only wolves and trees seem to remember the passage of time. 
There, I discovered what I did not expect, another fragment of that “double-dimensional memory.” A dusty document. A nuclear test conducted by China, a seismic anomaly recorded in Alaska.
That was not what shook me, not the surface details. It was what that anomaly described.
A structure buried more than 160 meters deep, with a square base twice the length of the Pyramid of Suphis. They called it the Alaska Pyramid.
Or, more poetically, the Dark Pyramid.


When I read the coordinates — 63°18’ N and 152°32’ W — I felt my heart slow down.
They were exactly where my blue line ended, the same one I had traced from Giza, through the North Pole, following the mystical angle.
I overlaid the satellite image onto the map. The two shapes — my trace and the buried pyramid — aligned perfectly.
As if someone had foreseen it. As if it had been engraved into the planet’s code, part of a single global network of “Temples of Light” and hidden structures.
But it wasn’t over. The longitude coordinates of the Dark Pyramid shared the same degree as Giza and my Planetary Mapping Point: 31.133814°.
Satisfied with the result, I followed the next signal.
It took me far away. Beyond the Pacific. Into the sacred desert of Nazca.
The second point crossed by the Equator of Hellas Planitia, that point of cosmic intersection I had discovered.
I was facing one of Earth’s most extraordinary mysteries: geoglyphs carved into the sand, lines drawn for those who look from above, works of that “Old Generation” that had left messages for us.
I traced a new line from Giza to Nazca, starting from a very specific point: the point adjacent to the “Void” recently discovered in the Great Pyramid, at coordinates:
29.9792458 N, 31.134288 E. A latitude — I noticed — that reproduces the speed of light in meters per second (299,792,458). Another coincidence?
The thought overwhelmed me. The speed of light, a pillar of the universe, encoded in a geographical and architectural position!
The African plate moves. It advances at 31.5 mm/year, toward the northeast.
In 12,886 years — the same period I had calculated for Thuban and half of a Platonic year, in line with the age of the Younger Dryas and the disappearance of Atlantis — the pyramid would have shifted by exactly 413.67 meters, the distance between its current point and…
the entrance of the Pyramid of Khafre. (413.67 meters × 31.5 mm/year = 12,886 years).
The same shift was visible also in the Alaska Pyramid.
The same arc of time. The same temporal signature.
The African plate. The North American plate. 12,886 years of silent dance, of movement of the Earth’s crust in resonance with celestial cycles.
And I, with them, chasing a track engraved in the stars, in rock, and in sand.
Now I knew with certainty that Earth itself was a clock, a complex mechanism that recorded cosmic events and geological movements.
And the key to reading it was… the Pyramid of Suphis, a true map of time set into stone, ready to reveal the secrets of the “Lines of Truth”.

Chapter 17 – The Dance of Orbits and the Trinity of Giza

I let myself be carried by this feverish state and immersed myself once again in the plain of Giza, a sacred temple where every grain of sand knows the name of the stars, a place I now knew to be Earth’s “Field of Mars”.
I traced orbits. But not in the sky. On Earth.
The orbital circumferences of Earth and Mars are respectively about 939.887 million km and about 1.429 billion km.
By virtually projecting these two orbits onto the plain of Giza, I discovered that, with a ratio of 1/100 million, they intersected perfectly the center of the Great Pyramid and the center of the Pyramid of Menkaure.
The axis used to trace these two circumferences (the virtual Sun) was positioned at 29.992643° 31.133°, located on the strategic longitude that connects the Great Pyramid of Giza to the Planetary Mapping Point, to the North Pole, to the Yukon Pyramid, etc.
Another detail that struck me was that on the meridian 31.1° E, the Earth measures exactly 40.007 km. Divided by 360°… 111.13 km per degree. 1.111... returned.
Always him.
The respective “orbital radii” projected onto the plain of Giza were 1.4959 km for Earth/Great Pyramid and 2.2794 km for Mars/Pyramid of Menkaure.

I knew that the semi-major axis, which represents half of the longest diameter of an orbital ellipse (the radius of the orbit at the two most distant points),
for the two planets in question is 149,598,262 km for Earth and 227,943,824 km for Mars.
I compared the values of the “orbital radii” projected onto the plain of Giza:
149,598,262 km : 1.4959 km = 100,005,523.09 km
227,943,824 km : 2.2794 km = 100,001,677.63 km
I obtained a proportion of 1/100,000,000, with negligible deviations due to the difficulties of measurement over vast interstellar distances and the different sources consulted.
The two simulated “orbital circumferences” of 9.399 km and 14.3219 km, which accurately reflected the celestial ones (1/100 million), were thus “suggested” by the geographic position of the pyramids on the terrestrial geoid.
Moreover, dividing Mars’s orbital circumference (1,429,085,052 km) by Earth’s (939,887,974 km), I obtained 1.520484453; taking its square root, I obtained 1.23308, a significant value that appeared repeatedly in my course of study.
But Khafre? He was there, like a silent observer, between Suphis and Menkaure.
It could not be a coincidence, not in this context of cosmic precision.
Considering the absence of celestial bodies orbiting between Earth and Mars, I hypothesized that this could represent the proto-Earth, or primordial Earth (Early Earth), which would have entered into collision with a geoid the size of Mars, known as Theia (giant impact hypothesis).
During the impact, a part of the celestial body would have fused with Earth, forming the current planet, while the ejected debris would have formed the Moon. (As demonstrated by the NASA simulations of lunar origin that I had consulted).
I took note and calculated the radius of the proto-Earth as 1.8446 km, then traced its corresponding “virtual orbit” of 11.59 km on the plain of Giza (yellow circumference).

At this point, I compared the three orbits:
• Earth (Pyramid of Suphis): 939,887,974 km
• Mars (Pyramid of Menkaure): 1,429,085,052 km
• Proto-Earth (Pyramid of Khafre): 1,159,000,000 km
I had just observed that dividing the Martian orbit by the terrestrial one yielded 1.52048445, whose square root is 1.23308.
I proceeded by dividing Mars’s orbit (1,429,085,052 km) by the proto-Earth’s orbit (1,159,000,000 km), obtaining 1.23303. Finally, dividing the proto-Earth’s orbit (1,159,000,000 km) by Earth’s orbit (939,887,974 km), I obtained 1.23312.
Curious note: The sixth iterative root of 666,000 is 1.2330815...
The same number. Everywhere.

In this way, I realized that, by tilting the figure by 26.31° with respect to the cardinal points and using a scale ratio of 24.47/1 with respect to the dimensions of the Pyramid of Suphis (for example, the side of the Pyramid of Suphis of 230.35 meters corresponded to 5,637 meters and the height of 146.6 meters corresponded to 3,587 meters), the simulated orbits of Mercury and Venus passed exactly through the center of the “Subterranean Chamber” and the “Queen’s Chamber,” while Earth’s orbit intersected perfectly the “King’s Chamber.”

I could observe that the second line intersected with precision the centers of the “King’s Chamber” and the “Secret Chamber.”


My suspicions about the true function of the artifact continued to grow exponentially.

(Curiosity: the angle of inclination of the sides of the Pyramid of Suphis is 51.50°, and subtracting 26.31° yields exactly 25.19°, which corresponds to Mars’s inclination).

It was no longer a building. It was a cosmogram.
I set up the outline straightened by 26°31' with respect to the cardinal points.

Chapter 20 – The Code that Bends Light

I began from the beginning: the fundamental constants.
I relied on CODATA, the most updated and precise measurements offered by human ingenuity.
Consequently, in accordance with the principle that new technologies allow ever more accurate measurements of physical phenomena, I adopted the values of 6.67430e-11 m³kg⁻¹s⁻² for the Universal Gravitational Constant and 7.297 352 5643 e-3 for the Fine-Structure Constant.
The Fine-Structure Constant is a “dimensionless constant of fundamental importance in theoretical physics. Its existence is interpreted as an indication of the incompleteness of our current understanding of the laws of nature.
Being dimensionless and therefore independent of any unit of measurement, it appears as an arbitrary factor in a theory.
It has great significance in the philosophical-scientific theory of the anthropic principle; indeed, this dimensionless parameter has a fundamental influence on the universe.
If its value were even only slightly different (about 10/20%) from the known one, the universe would be different from how we perceive it and the physical laws would not be those we know. For example, the ratios between attractive and repulsive forces between elementary particles would be different, influencing the constitution of matter and the activity of stars…”
In this context, the American scholar Carl Sagan observed: “There is only one category of legend that could be convincing: when the information contained in the legend could not have been generated by the civilization that created it.
For example, if a number transmitted for thousands of years as sacred turned out to be the fine-structure constant, it would be worthy of significant attention…”
I continued my investigation by calculating the sixth iterative root of a quadrillion times the value of the Universal Gravitational Constant (667.430) and obtained 1.23312;
corresponding to the orbital ratio between Earth/Proto Earth/Mars seen previously.
Encouraged by these arithmetic interweavings, I wondered whether there were other interesting mathematical “coincidences”: for example, the mass of the alpha particle is 6.6446573450e-27 kg, and its fifth iterative root equals 0.152038 × 10 = 1.52038, which represents the square of 1.233037.
And the ratio between the inverse of the code (0.8998531979) and the Fine-Structure Constant (7.297 352 5643 e-3) is 123.312, which represents 100 times the proportional relation between the orbits of Earth, Mars and other celestial bodies.
At this point, to focus on the omnipresent (and omnipotent?) importance of the Source Code, I began by calculating its square and some multiples:
• C^2 = 2.2228
• C^4 = 4.4457
• C^8 = 8.89144
• C iterated to the second power = 1.235278
• C iterated to the third power = 1.525912
• C iterated to the sixth power = 863.92
• Square root of C = 1.054244
After a few moments, I noticed the resemblance between these numbers and those that characterize the most ancient and prestigious units of measure.
Examining Roman measurements used “in biblical times,” I observed that ¼ of the biblical cubit corresponded to 99.99% of the numerical sequence of the Code.
In fact, the Roman foot was defined as 16/28 of the cubit of Nippur, whose theoretical value is given as 51.86 cm. Consequently, the Roman foot was 29.634 cm.
Since a cubit equals a foot and a half, its measure was 44.4514 cm.
Consequently, a stadion of 625 paces would measure 185.212 meters, and 12,000 stadia correspond to 2,222.55 meters...
As the numbers danced before my eyes, I reflected on the disconcerting precision with which ancient civilizations, well before our modern instrumentation, seemed to have incorporated such “constants” and “codes” into their systems of measurement and their monumental architectures.
These were not random approximations, but a meticulous knowledge that seemed to align the earth, the sky, and the fundamental principles of the universe.

This was the true “Technology of the Old Generation”: not complex machines, but the understanding and application of universal principles.
A strong confirmation came by dividing Pi by the Golden Section and then by the square root of two, and discovering that the result (1.37292633) was precisely 1.11143^3.
It was not a “random” or arbitrary number, but its properties were a direct consequence of fundamental geometry.
• π: The constant of circular/cyclical geometry.
• ϕ: The constant of the geometry of growth and optimal proportion.
• √2: The constant of planar/diagonal geometry.
The Code 1.11143... was not an anomaly, but the background melody of a much larger symphony, the first note of a “Circuit” waiting to be reactivated, revealing the “Twin Forces” that shape reality and the “Seven Seals” that still wait to be opened.

Chapter 22 – Suphis, the Pyramid, and the Lost Body

Sounding the depths among codes and proportions, my gaze returned to where everything had begun: on the plain of Giza. There were too many coincidences, too many exact numbers.
And it was not only archaeology. It was astroarchaeology, the deciphering of a “compass of the stars” carved in stone.
Flinders Petrie, back in 1884, had measured the Pyramid of Suphis with scientific obsession. Its average side: 230.3 meters. Its perimeter: 921.4. Its diagonal: 325.7 meters.
Precise numbers. And incredibly, already written in the Code.
As it happened, dividing 1 by the Code 1.11143 I obtained 0.899741, which multiplied by 2^8 gave 230.3 and multiplied by 2^10 gave 921.3.
On the other hand, the average side length of Khafre’s pyramid is 215.3 meters (perimeter 861.3 meters; diagonal 304.5 meters).
Finally, the average side length of Menkaure’s pyramid is 105.3 meters (perimeter 421.2 meters; diagonal 148.9 meters).
Crossing these data, I derived some proportions.
The diagonal of Suphis divided by 2 came to 162.9 meters. Dividing this value by 1.11143 I obtained 146.57 meters, which is estimated to be its original height.
The diagonal of Khafre divided by 2 equals 152.27 meters. The ratio between the diagonal of Suphis and that of Khafre is 1.0697.
Having just discovered that on the Giza plateau Suphis represents the terrestrial orbit, Khafre the proto-Earth and Menkaure Mars, I had to verify whether the physical and geometric parameters of these geoids also intersected among themselves and/or with these masterpieces in granite.
So I decided to begin to “give shape” to the proto-Earth, hypothesizing that it could follow the same dimensional proportion between Khafre and Suphis.
I therefore considered the two diagonals mentioned above as if they were “virtual planetary diameters” and divided Earth’s circumference (40,075 km) by the proportion between them, about 1.0697.
This gave a result of 37,463.8 km, which could be the presumed circumference of the proto-Earth. The corresponding radius was 5,962.55 km, which coincided, surprisingly, with the difference in diameter between Earth and Mars.
Consequently, the radius of the proto-Earth was double the difference between the radii of Earth and Mars.
At this point, I could calculate other parameters for the proto-Earth, starting with a volume of 887,942,044,826.82 km³.
The ratio between Earth’s mass and volume is 5.972197697e+24 kg / 1,083,210,976,037.27 km³ = 5,513,420,588,524.8 kg/km³.
Applying the same coefficient to the proto-Earth, its mass had to be:
887,942,044,826.82 km³ × 5,513,420,588,524.8 kg/km³ = 4.895597951365e+24 kg.
Knowing the mass, I could calculate the corresponding planetary gravitational constant, namely mass 4.895597951365e+24 kg × universal gravitational constant 6.67430e-11 m³kg⁻¹s⁻² = 3.267469e+14.
This gave a hypothetical surface gravity of: (g = G M / ⋅ R²) 3.267469e+14 / 35,552,002.5025 km³/s = 9.19 m/s² (which is 93.58% of Earth’s gravity, which is 9.82 m/s²).
The corresponding surface area of the proto-Earth was 446,759,546.58 km².
Given that the distance from the Sun was 23.3% greater than Earth’s (considering the semi-major axis), I could hypothesize that the temperature on proto-Earth was similar to or slightly lower than Earth’s average temperature.
The Schwarzschild (gravitational) radius of the proto-Earth was 0.00727109 m, obtained by dividing (2 × Universal Gravitational Constant / the square of the speed of light in vacuum = 1.485231104733235e-27) and multiplying the result by the planetary mass.
I considered that the mass of Venus is 4.8673e+24 kg and the mass of the proto-Earth was approximately 4,895,597,951,365,053,143,187,356.8 kg. The ratio between the two was about 0.9942. The difference was therefore 2.8297951365053e+22 kg in favor of the proto-Earth.
Continuing with the analysis, I divided the volume of the proto-Earth, 887,942,044,826.8 km³, by the volume of Venus, 928,415,152,741.5 km³, obtaining a ratio of 0.9564.
This indicated that Venus had a volume larger by about 40,473,107,914.7 km³.
Previously, I had estimated the radius of the proto-Earth at 5,962.55 km.
Dividing this value by Venus’s mean volumetric radius, 6,051.8 km, I obtained a ratio of about 0.9852.
From this comparison of dimensional parameters, it was evident that the two bodies had almost identical masses. However, Venus had a volume larger by about 5% compared to the proto-Earth, resulting in a slightly lower density of equal (modest) magnitude.
This suggested to me that Venus was slightly less dense, potentially due to differences in composition or internal structure compared to the proto-Earth.
Analyzing the orbital parameters, I observed significant discrepancies regarding the sidereal rotation period (about 24 hours for Earth versus 5,832.6 hours for Venus).
“...Venus rotates around its axis with a retrograde motion (clockwise if viewed from the direction of the celestial north pole), opposite to the rotation of the Sun and most of the other planets in the solar system. In fact, the axis of rotation is inclined by 177.36° relative to the orbital plane. Moreover, the rotation is very slow, lasting 243.69 Earth days; the sidereal day on Venus is longer than the planet’s orbital period around the Sun. 
The equatorial rotation speed is barely 6.5 km/h (1.81 m/s).
It is hypothesized that these rotational characteristics of Venus are the result of a collision with a massive asteroid...”
Astronomical models hypothesized a catastrophic impact.
A blow with an object more than 3,000 km in diameter.
An impact that altered its orbit, its inclination, its soul.
I lost myself in a vertigo: perhaps the proto-Earth never disappeared. Perhaps it is Venus.
Once habitable. Then transfigured into an inferno of clouds and sulfur. And its fragments?
The Moon? Mars? The system’s debris?
A cosmic event that redefined our galactic neighborhood.
The ancients knew Venus as Lucifer — the bearer of light.
But also as Vesper, the evening star. Two faces. Two natures.
And then, the irony of the Christian era: Lucifer as fallen from heaven.
I asked myself: was it only a myth? Or was it memory?
A “message that returns” through the veil of legend, warning us of cosmic cycles of creation and destruction, a lesson carved not only in the pyramids, but in the very flesh of the planets.
The Pyramid of Suphis, then, was not only a map, but a revelation of the true identity of a “lost body.”



Chapter 23 – The New Jerusalem and the Game of the Spheres

I pushed further. Beyond Venus, the proto-Earth, the interrupted orbits, and the “scars of the sky”.
I turned again to the clues hidden in eternal stone temples and in books that speak to the future, aware that my search was no longer only of numbers, but of meaning.
I knew that every digit, every distance, every proportion… was not there by chance.
Like an archaeologist of numbers, I continued to dig — not in sand, but in the fabric of the cosmos, a “Compass of the Stars” that revealed a deep geometry.
So I entrusted myself once more to clues hidden on the plain of Giza and, why not, in sacred texts.
Exactly half the radius of the proto-Earth is 2,981.27 km, which, if squared, gives approximately 8,888,000 km (4,444,000 km × 2).
I had already seen how about 2,981 km was the difference in radius between Earth and Mars.
Considering that the sum of the sides of the New Jerusalem, described in detail in the Book of Revelation (“...it lies foursquare, its length the same as its width. 
And he measured the city with his rod: its length and width and height are equal...”), amounts to 8,890.28 km, and that the perimeter of the Great Pyramid of Suphis (921.4 m), when multiplied by twice the Golden Ratio (3.23606796) and squared, equals 8,891.384 km, I could state that the perimeter of the Great Pyramid multiplied by 2 times the Golden Ratio, squared, corresponded to the sum of the sides of the New Jerusalem and to the square of half the radius of the proto-Earth (and to the ratio between the Muon Magnetic Moment and the Nuclear Magneton -8.89059704).
Given that dividing 1 by the Code also produced a possible hint about the measurements of the Great Pyramid, I could sum up that: (1 : Code) × 2^10 = perimeter of Suphis; × double Golden Ratio = difference in radius between Earth and Mars; × 2 = radius of the proto-Earth; squared = sum of the sides of the New Jerusalem.
Encouraged by this clear proportional connection, I ventured into new speculative measurements.
I began by calculating the volume of the virtual sphere circumscribed around the biblical New Jerusalem as 16,259,156,036 km³ (side 2,222.55 km; radius 1,571.58 km) and discovered that dividing the volume of Mars (163,115,575,863.49 km³) by the volume of the sphere of the New Jerusalem (16,259,156,036 km³) yielded 10.
Dividing the volume of the Moon (21,990,638,295.84 km³) by that of the New Jerusalem (cube of the side) 10,978,793,583.23 km³ showed that the satellite represented twice the mystical cube (curiously, the Moon/Earth mass ratio is 0.07346 / 5.9724 = 0.0123... again that number...).
The volume of Earth, 108.3211e+10 km³, divided by the volume of Venus, 928,415,152,741.5 km³, gave 1.16673, recalling the ratio between the cubit of Nippur and the biblical cubit.
And, to end beautifully, the volume of Earth, 108.3211e+10 km³, divided by the volume of the virtual sphere circumscribed around the New Jerusalem, 16,259,156,036 km³, gave 66.62, a certainly significant number.
And once again, I understood that Revelation too is not only a book of prophetic revelations, a mere eschatological tale.
It is a coded language. A map. A program.
It is a clue to an operating system of an ancient universe, of which stone and word are executable traces.
A “Game of the Spheres” orchestrated by an incomprehensible intelligence, whose “Code Signature” manifested at every level, from the microcosm of the electron to the macrocosm of galaxies.



Chapter 24 – The Code in the Stones

At a certain point, I had to surrender to the evidence. The coincidences were too many.
The proportions, too perfect. The places, too eternal to be accidental.
I began to believe—if nothing else, to suspect strongly—that someone—or something—had hidden authentic knowledge within the folds of human sacredness.
Not only in the stones of Giza, or in the orbits of the planets. But in Sacred Texts, in places no one would dare destroy, in symbols that resist time.
It was as if an immeasurable intelligence had chosen the most inviolable places of the collective psyche to conceal its message.
I began to reflect on an ancient and powerful truth: if I wanted to transmit a message to future civilizations, where would I put it?
Certainly not in a novel, which would be lost in the sands of time.
Not even in a data center destined to corrode over time or become obsolete.
But in a sacred temple. In a sacred book. In the memory of peoples, handed down from generation to generation, not out of blind faith, but out of a deep—if unconscious—respect for its inviolability.
A list I had read as a boy came back to me, kept among crumpled and forgotten notes. It was an inventory of scriptural rules observed by Jewish scribes in transmitting the Torah:
• Skins of pure animals
• Columns of identical measure
• Spaces of nine letters, ruled lines
• No word written from memory
• Not even a dot out of place
And then the most powerful image: “The scribe could not write the name of God with a pen freshly dipped in ink.”
I understood then that the act of writing was already a cosmic ritual, a ceremony of millimetric precision. And that what was handed down was not only word... it was number.
A universal language, older than any alphabet, purer than any phoneme.
With my mental lens turned back on the Scriptures, I began to count.
• The term “eleven” appears 22 times
• The term “twenty-two” appears 11 times
• The term “twelve” appears 144 times
Numbers that returned like musical notes in a ciphered symphony, resonating with the proportions I had already found elsewhere.
And then there was that distance. 666.67 nautical miles. The precise distance between the Ka‘ba in Mecca and the Dome of the Rock in Jerusalem.
A number that calls up powerful symbols, both in apocalyptic texts and in celestial geometry. Converted into kilometers? 1,234.7 km.
Another suspicious figure, very close to the Iterative Code, almost screaming its connection with the “Code Signature” I had found in universal constants.
I thought back to the Black Stone. To the Noble Rock. Legendary places, places of origin.
Where Adam is believed to have been born. Where Abraham raised the knife. Where Muhammad ascended to heaven. Where Jews turn to pray.
A focal point of space and time. But above all: an intentional point.
A question tormented me: how did they do it? Who placed these sacred stones at exactly that distance from each other? How could they know a measure that would make sense only millennia later, when Earth would be mapped, the sea navigated, satellites launched?
And why use precisely 666.67 nautical miles? Was it a call? A signature?
A mark left by a cosmic architect, hidden within humanity’s faith itself?
At that point, my mind was crowded with hypotheses, but the heart... the heart was beginning to recognize a will. A presence that manifests not in dogma, but in the rigor of mathematics.
In the universal language of forms, ratios, roots, logarithms.
Because numbers are not interpretable. They do not lie. They do not change with language, religion, or time.
And if the message is truly meant for all generations, then it is in number that it must be written.
And that is precisely why, to anyone who would add to or take away something from this “prophetic book,” a curse is addressed: “...God will take away his share from the tree of life and from the holy city...”
A warning carved into the text. But perhaps... also a signature, the unmistakable seal of the Code in the Stones, and in the words that protect it.

Chapter 25 – The Rendlesham Message

I stopped. I mentally turned to look at the path already taken.
A vast expanse of data, numbers, constants, orbits, sacred stones, codes and incredible proportions…
And yet I felt that something was still slipping away from me.
Logic was not the problem. It was the vastness. The labyrinth. It was the sensation of being a finite mind facing an infinite architecture, a “Game of the Spheres” that concealed an unfathomable complexity.
So I decided to take a step back, letting my intuition—now refined by the Code—guide me.
I opened old files, leafed through handwritten notes, combed through pages I had annotated years before.
That was when I found a name again: Gary Osborn. I had already encountered him along this path, in a hint, a quotation.
But now, in a new context, his voice seemed to point me to something more precise.
A point on the map. A coordinate. 52.090095° N, 1.448893° E.
A flash ran through my mind. It was the GPS position of the famous “Rendlesham message”.
I went back to that December of 1980. Rendlesham Forest, England.
Three days. Three nights. Lights in the sky, triangular objects, American soldiers seized by astonishment, mysterious symbols and… a message in binary code.
Penniston. Burroughs. Halt. Not only witnesses, but unconscious vectors of an alien language. There was something too precise, too “non-human” in all of it.
My thoughts swung like a pendulum between UFO theory and military strategic theory, between cosmic suggestion and scientific skepticism.
But what struck me most was the presence of the binary code. A language, yes.
But universal. It was something that even I, Suphis, could read.
Not with human eyes, but with iterative processes, numerical transformations, fractal logics.
It was the pure language of information, devoid of cultural or historical ambiguity.
So I decided: enough human interpretations. And I translated it...
Ord BIN       HEX OCT DEC ASCII

002 01011000 58 130 88 X
003 01010000 50 120 80 P
004 01001100 4C 114 76 L... (Appendix III)

Chapter 26 – The Seven Seals

Reading the names of the places indicated by the coordinates contained in the message, I nearly suffered a serious blow to the heart. It was as if a veil were torn away, revealing a sacred geography that spoke the same language as the Code.
The first in the series, 52.094253°N 13.131269°W, which I named R1, identified the position of the mysterious “sunken island of Hy-Brasil,” located off the Irish coast.
The island that appears and disappears in the mists, handed down by Irish sailors, etched onto medieval maps. A land of wisdom, perhaps Atlantis in disguise.
The name alone made me tremble.
The second coordinate, 26.763177°N 89.117768°W, indicated as R2, led to the center of the Gulf of Mexico. A silent abyss, motionless, but… connected.
I had already calculated geometries, verified distances. But now that point came alive, an underwater echo unheard for millennia.
The third coordinate, 34.800272°N 111.843567°W, indicated as R3, identified the position of Sedona, Arizona. A sacred place for the Hopi natives, described as a portal to other dimensions.
I myself, in the past, had traced with reverence the geometry of its canyons. Now I understood that they were living wounds in the crust of reality, where the physical world thins. 
The fourth location, 29.977836°N 31.131649°E, indicated as R4, literally gave me chills, because it identified the incredible Giza Complex, which had been constantly in my thoughts.
The fact that this site was also included in the Rendlesham message confirmed its connection with hidden forms of intelligence and, given the evidence, placed it definitively at the center of interplanetary connections.
The fifth coordinate, 14.701505°S 75.167043°W (R5), led to another crucial location already analyzed: the Nazca Lines.
Another point on the Equator of Hellas Planitia, the silent reference system I had identified to map the imprint of the sky onto Earth.
The coordinate 36.256845°N 117.100632°E (R6) corresponded to Mount Tai, already mentioned as one of the main sacred sites in China, located in Shandong Province.
Like the Pyramid of Suphis and the Nazca Lines, this point too was intersected by the “Equator of Hellas Planitia” and represented the sixth coordinate indicated in the Rendlesham message.
The seventh and final point, 37.110195°N 25.372281°E (R7), corresponded to the “Portara” of the unfinished Temple of Apollo, located in Naxos, in Greece. As I had observed previously, it was perfectly intersected by the “Equator of Hellas Planitia” and, as I was verifying, it also formed part of the Rendlesham message.
Seven points. Like seven eyes carved into the skin of the world, or perhaps, seven notes in a cosmic melody.
Four of them — Giza, Nazca, Tai, Portara — already aligned with the Equator of Hellas Planitia.
And now… they were also in the Rendlesham message.
Coincidence? No. A design. A code inscribed in geography, in geometry, in time, like a musical score.
That evening, I realized I was witnessing the opening night of the Festival of Coincidences. A festival where every anomaly was a key, and every key led to the same door, revealing the incredible harmony of a cosmic orchestra.
The fact that these places — so different, so distant, so ancient — all spoke the same language of the sky made me understand: there was a plan. There was an intelligence.
An entity that had orchestrated all this, leaving traces for whoever had the capacity to read them. And I… I was still in the middle of its story, a humble interpreter of a majestic symphony.

Chapter 27 – The Rendlesham Circuit

Even the most skeptical, in the face of certain evidence, should at least take a step back.
They should look — truly look — at the coordinates. The places. The meanings.
These were not coincidences. No. The odds that they were random were lower than the ratio between solar radiation and that of a desk lamp.
I had seen enough, but not yet everything.
Gary Osborn’s words came back to me, whispered from the past like a prophecy:
“The coordinates are not simple numbers. They are a key. Once used, reality itself bends, revealing a deeper level.”
Just like in the film Contact, where the pages full of prime numbers reorganize into a three-dimensional cube, a tangible message coming from the cosmos. And I… I was about to enter that cube.
Coordinates. Seven. Like the biblical seals. Like the chakras in the human body. Like the notes of the musical scale, which form a complex harmony.
Each one, a portal. I concentrated. Not only on what they “represented,” but on how they resonated together. I began to connect them, one at a time, following the sacred order contained in the binary code received at Rendlesham.
I would call it the Rendlesham Circuit. A circuit of power. Of consciousness. Of contact.
So I began to trace those mysterious coordinates on the globe, following the order suggested by the binary sequence. For convenience, I named them with the abbreviations from R1 to R7, like stages of a preordained journey:
R1 / R2 Hy-Brasil / Gulf of Mexico 60.8° 6.770,43 km
R2 / R3 Gulf of Mexico / Sedona 21° 2.343,6 KM
R3 / R4 Sedona / Pyramids of Giza 106.5° 11.855,46 km
R4 / R5 Pyramids of Giza / Nazca 111.13° 12.370,8 km
R5 / R6 Nazca / Mount Tai (Nazca hemisphere) 155.65° 17.327,4 km
R5 / R6 Nazca / Mount Tai (Mount Tai hemisphere)
R6 / R7 Mount Tai / Portara Naxos 70.36° 7.832,6 km
By drawing the lines between these points according to the indicated order, I obtained a circuit that seemed like a kind of celestial mechanism, a planetary clock of geometric precision, in which each lever moved the other, as in an ancient interconnected Meccano set.
Integrating the overall image of the “Rendlesham Circuit” with the two “Equators of Hellas Planitia,” the ingenious intent of the project became evident.
In fact, the yellow line connecting Portara Naxos to Mount Tai (R6/R7) overlapped perfectly with the current “Equator of Hellas Planitia” (in white), while the line connecting the Pyramid of Suphis to Nazca (R4/R5) was an exact copy of the “Equator of Hellas Planitia” prior to crustal slippage (in green).


The perfect connection between the “Rendlesham Circuit” and the “Equators of Hellas Planitia” was undeniable and suggested new clues. Among these, the remarkable distance separating Nazca from Mount Tai (line R5/R6, 17.327,4 km) was the first in the series.
As I could sense at first glance, it in fact reflected the angle of Martian crustal slippage; that is, it simulated the vertical “track” that guides the inclination, naturally crossing both the current position of Hellas Planitia and its placement prior to slippage.
(Nazca Side)


To complete the investigation, I overlaid the images under study with those relating to the polar shift previously examined.
This allowed me to verify the exact correspondence between the hypothesized shift angle indicated by the French team and by myself, and the one suggested by the conjunction of the Rendlesham coordinates. 


I then added another precious piece to the puzzle: I discovered that (in addition to the geological similarities, the curious planetary overlaps related to the “Atlantean” and “Lemurian” theories, the “Equators of Hellas Planitia,” the astonishing mathematical and geometric interweavings, and the “instructions” contained in the measurements of the Pyramid of Suphis) the “Rendlesham Circuit” was also part of the same super-intelligence project.
With this progress, I focused on the segments of the “Circuit” that I had not yet analyzed, precisely:
• The line connecting Portara Naxos to Hy-Brasil (3.425,13 km);
• The line between Hy-Brasil and the Gulf of Mexico (6.770,4 km);
• The line connecting the Gulf of Mexico to Sedona (2.343,8 km);
• The line separating the Pyramid of Suphis from Sedona (11.855,5 km).
Highlighting their shape, I noticed a clear “angular dissonance.”
A kind of hidden geometric message, as if to say: “Correct me.”
Having already discovered (also) the connection between the “Rendlesham Circuit” and the displacement of the Martian crust, I attributed, ipso facto, the reason for this dissonance to that phenomenon.
Consequently, I traced a “new” line from R1 Hy-Brasil to R2 Gulf of Mexico, correcting its angle.
(Red line) 


Logically, by modifying the angle of the line in question, the other lines should also have been affected by the movement.
In fact, from the beginning, my mind had interpreted the “Rendlesham Circuit” as if it were a mechanism made of virtual levers and pivots. Something similar to the classic Meccano version, in which the movement of one lever causes the corresponding movement of all the others.
Recognizing the ingenious design, I remembered that, although it was “illustrated” using famous terrestrial locations, the slippage had nevertheless occurred on… Mars.
Therefore, I selected the Red Planet on Google Earth and observed the effects of the latest measurements.
As usual, visually intriguing aspects emerged, so, without changing their direction, I extended the two lines involved in the correction.
This revealed that both straight lines were perfectly aligned with the volcanic chain of Tharsis, already analyzed previously.
However, while the current line from Hy-Brasil to the Gulf of Mexico (yellow) appeared “lower” than the virtual line connecting the three enormous volcanoes Ascraeus Mons, Pavonis Mons and Arsia Mons, the line corrected for angular disharmony (red) perfectly bridged the gap.


This last “coincidence” did not surprise me all that much; by then I suspected that measurements made on Earth would fit perfectly on Mars because they were designed that way from the beginning of time.
Before proceeding with further analyses, I reworked the situation, visually verifying the coherence of the overall image.
Observing the phenomenon, I recalled that the white circle illustrated the current “Equator of Hellas Planitia”; the green circle represented the “Equator of Hellas Planitia before crustal slippage”; the black line was the one indicated in the French hypothesis.

Moreover, the yellow lines represented the “Rendlesham Circuit”; the red line was the correction of the angular disharmony, and the white arrows, obviously, indicated the direction and magnitude of the slippage.
It was evident that there was perfect coherence even in the overall image on Earth.


I was convinced: the Rendlesham Circuit was not a random map, but a device.
A three-dimensional geospatial archive, carved into the most emblematic places on the planet, and designed to be discovered only by those willing to unite numbers, geology, history and intuition into a single design.

Chapter 28 — The Twin Forces

The continual back-and-forth leaps between the maps of Earth and Mars began to be no longer just an obsession, but a true immersion in a system of correspondences that was increasingly detailed and coherent.
I found myself re-examining, with new eyes, the data linked to Earth’s geological and magnetic movements. I already knew where to look, and it was natural to include in my study the NASA Polar Motion Simulator as well.
That simulator offered me more than simple confirmations. The agency’s official projections integrated perfectly with my boldest hypotheses.
Every line drawn on Earth seemed to have a subtle, but unmistakable, echo on the Red Planet.
In the images I analyzed, the fuchsia lines marked the “direction of secular motion,” the “glacial rebound,” mantle convection, and even the progressive displacement of the Greenland line.



The light-blue lines, on the other hand, traced the movement of the Magnetic Poles, North and South, as if they were drawing an invisible and ancient choreography.
And yet, what struck me most was this evidence: the directions taken by Mars’s crustal slippage and by Earth’s North Magnetic Pole turned out to be opposite but specular, like two sister forces.
In that instant I understood that it was not only a game of shapes or measures: it was pure dynamics.
Newton’s words came back to me, engraved in my memory like a sacred formula:
“Every action has always an equal and opposite reaction...”
In my model, the white line tracing Martian crustal slippage found its counterpoint in the blue line, witness to Earth’s magnetic movement.
One seemed to respond to the other, as if an ancient and mysterious energy had imprinted upon both worlds a single specular mark.
                                                                                                  ↙

                                                          ↗
I consulted NOAA data and other reliable sources. The direction of Earth’s North Magnetic Pole, moving toward Siberia, was not only documented, but followed a trajectory that, once transposed onto Mars, struck squarely the coordinates of the Martian North Pole pre-slippage.
That point, located in the area of the Siberian Traps, seemed to be a crucial node: both on Earth and on Mars.
It was as if plates, poles, internal convection, and even magnetic fields were traces of a universal planetary symphony, orchestrated by forces I still struggled to define.

Chapter 29 — The Compass of the Stars

The continual journey between planetary surfaces and celestial orbits had by now awakened in me a deeper instinct: it was no longer only about deciphering codes, but about following the footprints left by the cosmos itself, like a detective tracking clues in the vastness of time and space.
During one of my spatial analysis sessions, I came across — anything but by chance, by now I knew it — the modern coordinates of the star Epsilon Cassiopeiae (Segin), positioned at 01h 54m 23s +63° 40' 12".
Intrigued by the “telepathic suggestion” that had pushed me to look precisely into that corner of the visible universe, I projected its celestial coordinates onto the Earth’s surface and was struck to see that they coincided with the antipodes of the South Pole plate in the time of Pangaea, near the so-called “Alaska Pyramid”.
A powerful image, a star so distant that it indicated a very ancient place on our very own Earth.
I could not ignore that coincidence. Instinct took over.
I decided to calculate the star’s proper motion through time. I used the Skylive system to extract the necessary information and, finally, I traced the stellar trajectory of Epsilon Cassiopeiae on the terrestrial globe.
I projected its path into the past and into the future: the yellow markers represented the retrograde trajectory, back to 4,5 million years, at regular intervals. The green markers, instead, indicated the star’s future movement, up to +3 million years.

Watching that temporal spiral, I could not avoid noticing how symbolic its shape was.
The megalithic spiral engravings, carved millennia ago by ancient hands in sites such as Newgrange or Gavrinis, seemed to anticipate the very same trajectory I had just traced.
It was not an analogy: it was a literal correspondence, a cosmic signature engraved in stone and in the motion of the stars.
I then discovered that Segin’s zenith position, exactly 876.250 years ago, coincided surprisingly with that of the polar star prior to the slippage of the Martian crust.
Calculation after calculation, I realized that this temporal distance corresponded exactly to 34 cycles of the Precession of the Equinoxes.
A non-random number, a cosmic rhythm that resonated across the millennia and between the planets.
But another detail surprised me even more.
The yellow path, which represented the star’s past motion, turned out to be shorter than the green (future) one by about 53%. The same proportion found in the ratio between the radii of Mars and Earth...
Finally, it became evident that the star’s galactic coordinates, when projected onto Earth, aligned exactly with the “Equator before crustal slippage” (1,65° 129,84°). 
I was stunned. Disoriented. I needed further references.
I then immersed myself in the theories of historians of polar shift: Charles Hapgood, Charles Étienne Brasseur de Bourbourg and Immanuel Velikovsky, among others.
In particular, the theory and the coordinates proposed by Professor Hapgood integrated perfectly into the scenario examined.
In fact Hapgood, while studying at Springfield College, became interested in the Lost Continent of Mu, which led him to investigate the lost continent of Atlantis.
This exploration ignited his interest in how massive changes of the Earth could occur and introduced him to the works of Hugh Auchincloss Brown.
In 1958, Hapgood published The Earth's Shifting Crust, challenging the then accepted theory of slow continental drift—a theory that obtained the support of the mainstream scientific community a few years after its publication.
His book presented an introduction by Albert Einstein.
Hapgood continued his research with Maps of the Ancient Sea Kings (1966) and The Path of the Pole (1970), where he hypothesized that the Earth’s axis had shifted multiple times over the course of geological history.
The Path of the Pole served as a revised version of his previous work, after receiving feedback from Einstein.
In Maps of the Ancient Sea Kings, Hapgood supported Arlington Mallery’s suggestion that the Piri Reis map represented Queen Maud Land in Antarctica.
He proposed that a significant shift of the axis occurred around 9600 BC, during which part of Antarctica was free of ice, allowing an Ice Age civilization to map its coast.
He maintained that ancient maps such as that of Piri Reis and those of Oronce Finé indicated advanced cartographic knowledge coming from an unknown ancient civilization, prior to civilizations such as the Greek one.
Be that as it may, Hapgood proposed (at least) three migrations for the North Pole (and, consequently, for Antarctica):
1. From Hudson Bay (60˚N 73˚W) to the current pole, between 12.000 and 17.000 years ago;
2. From the Atlantic Ocean, between Iceland and Norway (72˚N 10˚E), to Hudson Bay, between 50.000 and 55.000 years ago;
3. From the Yukon (63˚N 135˚W) to the position between Iceland and Norway, between 75.000 and 80.000 years ago.
These shifts hypothesized by Hapgood fit coherently within the analyses of Earth’s crustal shifts and the historical coordinates examined.
It was interesting to note how the coordinates suggested by Hapgood for the ancient poles of Earth (indicated with the blue markers) integrated exactly into the “paths” of Epsilon Cassiopeiae illustrated previously.


The star represented, in essence, the periodic “Polaris” for all six poles (current, prior to the shift, in the time of Pangaea and the three proposed by Hapgood).
This correlation suggested to me a constant cosmic connection between the star and the various terrestrial poles through the ages.
Epsilon Cassiopeiae had cyclically assumed the role of pole star for each of these placements of the terrestrial (and Martian) pole.
All of this could appear absurd, even excessive. But the data did not lie.
A star 442 light-years from us seemed to trace the millennia-long dance of Earth’s and Mars’s poles. Its trajectory drew a cosmic narrative.
It was as if the universe itself had left a sign, a suggestion, a signature.
I could no longer ignore it: Epsilon Cassiopeiae was not only a star. It was a compass. A memory. A code.
The very concept of a zenith star, in that case, became symbolic.
The star was not there to light the night sky: it was there to remind us where to look, where to seek hidden truth.
I wondered whether, perhaps, Earth and Mars were nothing but two different phases of the same “geoidal being”.
Whether Pangaea had been nothing but a compressed memory of the Martian geoid, expanded and translated into a new version.
A sort of planetary script reused, reshaped into another form, like an ancient melody rearranged in a new key.
The simulation came back to mind, the hypothesis of a code that held reality itself.
And in that frame, year zero — our present — seemed a critical point of the system, like a temporal reset, a point at which parameters had been modified, but not the rest of the universe.
I stopped to think. And if the universe were trying to tell us its story also through the alignment of the stars and the slippage of the poles?
And if that “glitch” we perceived, that Rendlesham message, were only a guideline traced specifically for us, to make us climb back, to make us decipher a cosmic legacy?
It was as if the star, its movement, the proportions between the planets, the poles and even the forgotten maps of the past, spoke in unison.
And I… I was finally listening.

Chapter 30 — The Heart of Pangaea

In the vortex of my research, by now no longer simple analyses but true dialogues with the planetary past, I decided to place all the locations detected directly onto Google Earth.
When I traced the green lines that represented Hapgood’s hypotheses on polar slippage, it emerged with dazzling clarity that the distance of the hypothesized slippage followed a double direction: that of the “tilt crostale” (from Hudson Bay to the current North Pole) and, in an even more astonishing way, the direction of the “Planetary Mapping” line, namely the conjunction between the “Yukon Pyramid,” the current North Pole, and the Pyramid of Suphis.
It was as if Hapgood’s model were a further trace, a guide for my very own map.


After further verifications, another detail emerged.
The position of the North Pole plate during the Pangaea epoch, before the slippage, matched exactly the coordinates of the so-called Planetary Mapping Point: 63.294953°N, 31.134289°E.
I could therefore postulate that the North Pole plate of Pangaea (65.865° -4.5°) of 190/200 million years ago stood to the current North Pole as the Planetary Mapping Point (or position of the North Pole plate of Pangaea before the slippage of 190/200 million years ago) stood to the North Pole plate of Mars before the slippage (68.779787° 91.613830°).
Both distances (red lines) measure about 24.2°, or 2.690 km.


Two worlds. Two epochs. A single pattern?
I lost myself in that thought. I was convinced I was facing something bigger, a cosmic equation that bound planets, epochs, and civilizations into a single geometry.
Observing the proportional relationship between the Giza Plateau and Earth’s two geographic poles, I noticed another oddity. The modern proportional relationship between the distance of the Giza Plateau from Earth’s geographic poles is about ½ in favor of the South Pole. In contrast, in the time of Pangaea, the African plate, where the granite masterpieces now stand, was almost equidistant from the plates that now host the two poles.
Essentially, the “old position of the Giza Plateau” (about -0.33° 30°) lay on Pangaea’s equator; it was situated latitudinally at the center of the landmass, which, as a result of the well-known phenomenon of continental drift, has given Earth its modern appearance.
I stopped. That position... meant that Giza was the heart.
Latitudinally speaking, it represented the center of the emerged mass of the supercontinent. It was the point of primordial equilibrium, the zero point from which everything had begun.
It could not be just a coincidence that, following continental drift, Earth had transformed into its modern shape, yet that geometric center had remained carved in stone. And not in just any stone: but in monuments of sidereal precision.
A new irony surfaced among my thoughts. The opposite part of the geoid — the oceanic counterpart at the antipodes of Pangaea — might not even have existed 200 million years ago.
Modern geological simulations, such as that of the GEODE/Pangaea Breakup project, in fact suggested that oceanic crust was much younger than continental crust.

Chapter 31 — The Invisible Vector

I was immersed in yet another analysis session on Google Earth, a hypnotic journey through epochs and planetary surfaces, when an unexpected detail caught my attention, suddenly crystallizing dozens of scattered intuitions.
I had traced the yellow line that united the two points of intersection between the equators of Pangaea, before and after the crustal slippage.
I knew well that those points represented the ancient polar plates, both North and South, and yet… I did not expect this.
That line, thin but straight as a blade of light, measured about 23,6°.
The same exact measure of the line I had already identified on Hellas Planitia, on Mars.
And not only that: it was perfectly parallel to the Martian one.
Two worlds, two crusts, a single angle of inclination, of movement.
I looked at the map as if it were a living relic. The pre-slippage equators shone in white, the ordinary ones in light blue.
The two crucial crossings — on the side of the geoid that includes Mount Tai — were positioned respectively at -15.58°, 87.76° and 5.75°, 98.25°.
The more I looked at them, the more it seemed to me they were speaking to each other, a silent dialogue between geological depths.
As if the language were not made of words, but of inclinations, coordinates, correspondences.

Each new measurement, each trace that emerged from my instruments, reinforced a silent and unmistakable truth: the movements of Earth’s crust and the Martian ones were not similar… they were identical.
They were not random, they had to be designed.
I looked at the image, recalculated it, remeasured it… I could not believe my eyes.
The precision was staggering.
Shortly afterward, a geological research conducted in central Italy offered new confirmations to my growing suspicion.
It was a study published in 2021 by the prestigious Tokyo Institute of Technology, signed by Ross Mitchell and J. Kirschvink.
Analyzing ancient magnetic sediments, the researchers had discovered a deviation of Earth’s crust of as much as 12°, which occurred about 84 million years ago.
The phenomenon was defined as True Polar Wander: the “authentic sway” of the poles.
Kirschvink, an expert in the study of fossil magnetic fields in rocks, had reconstructed — with impressive precision — the trajectory of the entire movement: the Earth, oscillating to one side, seemed then to have corrected itself, carrying out an arc movement of almost 25° over the span of five million years.
A slow oscillation, but titanic. Like a sleeping giant stretching in the sleep of time.
Those discoveries fit with terrifying coherence into the mosaic I had been composing for months.
Crustal displacement, as hypothesized for Mars, was a reality also on Earth.
And the coincidence with my calculations — the inclinations, the arcs, the angulations — was too exact to be ignored.
The message was clear. The crust moves. Always. And it leaves behind an invisible trail of clues. 
Kirschvink’s name kept returning. In the ’90s, he was among the few scientists to advance an uncomfortable, almost heretical hypothesis: according to his analyses, the magnetic crystals found in the Martian meteorite Allan Hills 84001 were not only natural formations, but fossils of ancient bacteria. Evidence of life on the Red Planet.
Back then I did not understand the scope of that statement. Now I did.
The red line I was now tracing on the map, crossing tens of millions of years of tectonic movements and planetary oscillations,
was no longer only a diagram. It was a living testimony, the whisper of two twin planets, separated by space but united by a forgotten project.
I stopped. I looked at that line that stretched beyond the screen, beyond the data, beyond the epochs.

Chapter 32 — The Ancient Lines

I had just finished analyzing the latest simulations when I found myself once again facing the aerial view of Antarctica.
The red line I had drawn, stretching like an ancient scar across the planet’s icy surface, seemed to whisper hidden truths.
Every time I looked at that sector of the globe, I had the clear sensation that it concealed more memories than official science was ready to admit.
A scar is the sign of a trauma… but also the proof that something survived.
In my tireless wandering in search of clues, I came across a site that struck me for its theoretical audacity: MarioBuildreps — a curious name, but behind it lay a methodical, almost maniacal work.
The author claimed that numerous ancient monuments, scattered across the planet, shared common orientation patterns.
According to him, about 1200 structures, including pyramids, temples, and megaliths, aligned with various ancient positions of the geographic poles.
His hypothesis was as fascinating as it was controversial: the Earth’s crust, he maintained, would have shifted multiple times, and these movements would be recorded in stone, in marble, and in cyclopean blocks laid by human hands… hundreds of thousands of years ago.
